    var seen = {};
    return a.filter(function(item) {
        return seen.hasOwnProperty(item) ? false : (seen[item] = true);
    });
}

  <script data-cfasync="false">
   function uuidProfileCall() {
			var rootUrl = 'https://api.parsely.com/v2/profile?apikey=wtop.com';
			var uuid = '&uuid=' + PARSELY.config.parsely_site_uuid;
			var requestUrl = rootUrl + uuid + '&url=' + window.location.href;
			jQuery.ajax({
				url: requestUrl,
				dataType: "jsonp"
			});
		}

		if (typeof PARSELY == 'object') {
			var oldonload = PARSELY.onload;
			if (typeof PARSELY.onload != 'function') {
				PARSELY.onload = uuidProfileCall
			}
			else {
				PARSELY.onload = function () {
					if (oldonload) {
						oldonload();
					}
					uuidProfileCall();
				};
			}
		}

		else {
			PARSELY = {
				onload: uuidProfileCall
			}
		}
  </script>

   var renderInvisibleReCaptcha = function() {

         (function(frm){

                'sitekey': '6LcbxrMUAAAAAAeoG7YSHf3BcMLOUgTw90RkVS--', 'size': 'invisible', 'badge' : 'bottomright',

					if((null !== cf7SubmitElm) && (typeof jQuery != 'undefined')){jQuery(frm).submit();grecaptcha.reset(holderId);return;}

                    function downloadComScoreAtOnload() {

  <!-- Parsely Conversions -->
  <script defer="" type="text/javascript">
   /** Parse.ly Conversions Standard (v0.1.1) Start **/
                    (function () {
                        'use strict';

                        var conversionConfigs = {
                            "customer": {
                                "apikey": "wtop.com"
                            },
                            "conversions": [
                                {
                                    "type":
                                        "Newsletter Signup",
                                    "selector": "form#sailthru-form-content-homepage",
                                    "event":
                                        "submit",
                                },
                                {
                                    "type":
                                        "Subscription",
                                    "selector": "form#sailthru-form-content-widget",
                                    "event":
                                        "submit",
                                },
                            ]
                        };

                        var conversionEventQueue = [];
                        var conversionMethodsAvailable = function () {
                            if (!window.PARSELY.loaded) {
                                return false;
                            } else if (!Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(window.PARSELY, "conversions")) {
                                return false;
                            } else {
                                return true;
                            }
                        };
                        var captureParselyConversion = function (methodName) {
                            if (conversionMethodsAvailable()) {
                                window.PARSELY.conversions[methodName]();
                            } else {
                                conversionEventQueue.push(methodName);
                            }
                        };
                        var initQueueHandler = function (q) {
                            var existingOnload = window.PARSELY.onload;
                            var flushQueue = function (q) {
                                for (var i = 0; i < q.length; i++) {
                                    window.PARSELY.conversions[q[i]]();
                                }
                            };
                            if (existingOnload === undefined) {
                                window.PARSELY._onload = function() { flushQueue(q); };
                                Object.defineProperty(window.PARSELY, "onload", {
                                    get: function() { return this._onload },
                                    set: function(x) {
                                        var existing = this._onload;
                                        this._onload = function() {
                                            existing();
                                            x();
                                        };
                                        return this._onload;
                                    }
                                });
                            } else {
                                window.PARSELY.onload = function () {
                                    existingOnload();
                                    flushQueue(q);
                                };
                            }
                        };
                        var conversionFnMap = {
                            "Lead Capture": function () { captureParselyConversion("trackLeadCapture"); },
                            "Subscription": function () { captureParselyConversion("trackSubscription"); },
                            "Newsletter Signup": function () { captureParselyConversion("trackNewsletterSignup"); }
                        };
                        var currentUrlIsAllowed = function (conversion) {
                            if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(conversion, "allowedUrls")) {
                                var loc = window.location;
                                for (var i = 0; i < conversion.allowedUrls.length; i++) {
                                    if (locMatchesUrl(loc, conversion.allowedUrls[i])) {
                                        return true;
                                    }
                                }
                                return false;
                            }
                            return true;
                        };
                        var locMatchesUrl = function (loc, urlToCheck)  {
                            var locUrl = loc.host + loc.pathname + loc.search;
                            var urlToCheckSplit = urlToCheck.split('//');
                            var urlToCheckPathName = urlToCheckSplit[urlToCheckSplit.length - 1];
                            if (locUrl.indexOf(urlToCheckPathName) !== -1) {
                                return true;
                            }
                        };

                        var retryInterval = 100;
                        var maxRetries = 100;
                        var initParselyConversions = function (configs) {
                            var results = [];
                            if (!conversionMethodsAvailable()) {
                                initQueueHandler(conversionEventQueue);
                            }
                            for (var i = 0; i < configs.conversions.length; i++) {
                                results.push(processConversionConfig(configs.conversions[i]));
                            }
                            return results;
                        };
                        var processConversionConfig = function (conversion) {
                            if (!currentUrlIsAllowed(conversion)) {
                                return;
                            }
                            if (conversion.event === "piano") {
                                return addPianoListeners(conversion);
                            } else if (conversion.event === "load") {
                                conversionFnMap[conversion.type]();
                                return ["onload"];
                            } else {
                                return addStandardListeners(conversion);
                            }
                        };
                        var addStandardListeners = function (conversion) {
                            var callback = conversionFnMap[conversion.type];
                            var elements = document.querySelectorAll(conversion.selector);
                            if (elements.length === 0 && conversion.poll === true) {
                                setTimeout(addStandardListeners, retryInterval, conversion);
                            }
                            for (var j = 0; j < elements.length; j++) {
                                elements[j].addEventListener(conversion.event, function(){callback();});
                            }
                            return elements
                        };
                        var addPianoListeners = function (conversion) {
                            var callback = conversionFnMap[conversion.type];
                            if (window.tp === undefined) {
                                setTimeout(addPianoListeners, retryInterval, conversion);
                            }
                            else {
                                window.tp.push(["addHandler", conversion.selector || "checkoutComplete", function(){
                                    callback();
                                }]);
                                return conversion.type;
                            }
                        };

                        function main () {
                            var retries = 0;
                            var parselyInterval = setInterval(function(){
                                retries++;
                                if (window.PARSELY) {
                                    clearInterval(parselyInterval);
                                    return initParselyConversions(conversionConfigs);
                                } else if (retries >= maxRetries) {
                                    console.warn("Parse.ly Conversions Standard snippet couldn't load because the Parse.ly tracker never loaded.");
                                    clearInterval(parselyInterval);
                                }
                            }, retryInterval);
                        }

                        return main();

                    }());

                    /** Parse.ly Conversions Standard End **/
  </script>
  <!-- /Parsely Conversions -->

  <script defer="" type="text/javascript">
   var _qevents = _qevents || [];

                    function downloadQuantcastAtOnload() {
                        var elem = document.createElement('script');
                        elem.src = (document.location.protocol == "https:" ? "https://secure" : "http://edge") + ".quantserve.com/quant.js";
                        elem.async = true;
                        elem.type = "text/javascript";
                        var scpt = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
                        scpt.parentNode.insertBefore(elem, scpt);
                    }

                    _qevents.push({
                            qacct:"p-sgZGQjSAzUNrD"
                    });
                    if (window.addEventListener)
                        window.addEventListener("load", downloadQuantcastAtOnload, false);
                    else if (window.attachEvent)
                        window.attachEvent("onload", downloadQuantcastAtOnload);
                    else window.onload = downloadQuantcastAtOnload;
  </script>
